;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;-
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
Trigger Aragonese_Admiral_trigger
	WhenToTest PostBattle
	Condition IsAdmiral
	and	FactionType aragon
	and	not FactionwideAncillaryExists Aragonese_Admiral
	and	not HasAncType Politics
	and	Attribute NavalCommand >= 3

	AcquireAncillary	Aragonese_Admiral	chance	100

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;-
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
Trigger Aragonese_Chancellor_trigger
	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
	Condition AgentType = priest
	and	not IsFactionLeader
	and	not IsFactionHeir
	and	FactionType aragon
	and	not HasAncType Politics
	and	not FactionwideAncillaryExists Aragonese_Chancellor
	and	Attribute Loyalty >= 5

	AcquireAncillary	Aragonese_Chancellor	chance	100

	and	FactionType aragon
	and	not FactionwideAncillaryExists Aragonese_Royal_notary

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;-
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
Trigger King_of_Aragon_trigger
	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
	Condition IsFactionLeader
	and	FactionReligion catholic
	and	Attribute Command >= 2
	and	Attribute Authority >= 4
	and	not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists King_of_Aragon
	and	EndedInSettlement
	and	SettlementName Jaca_Province

	AcquireAncillary	King_of_Aragon	chance	100

	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
	Condition IsGeneral
	and	not IsFactionLeader
	and	not IsFactionHeir
	and	FactionType aragon
	and	Attribute Loyalty >= 4
	and	Attribute Piety >= 4
	and	I_TurnNumber >= 520
	and	not HasAncType politics
	and	not FactionwideAncillaryExists Late_Aragonese_Royal_Chamberlain
	and	EndedInSettlement
	and	SettlementName Jaca_Province

	AcquireAncillary	Late_Aragonese_Royal_Chamberlain	chance	100

Trigger Order_of_the_stole_trigger
	WhenToTest PostBattle
	Condition IsGeneral
	and	FactionType aragon
	and	not IsFactionLeader
	and	not IsFactionHeir

	and	Attribute Loyalty >= 3
	and	not HasAncType Security
	and	I_TurnNumber >= 646

	AcquireAncillary	Order_of_the_stole	chance	10
